Chapter 1 : Shrestiab Pecp
---

Shrestiab Pecp was a female halfling that lived in Donson.
Donson was a nice town. Nondescript, for now. Shrestiab had a
mentor, named Alujaldwo Smimg. Also nondescript. Alujaldwo tells
Shrestiab 'I call you to adventure!'. But Shrestiab says 'No
sir! I refuse the call to adventure. I want to stay here in
Donson and smoke pipes at Tosci's Power Converters and Pipe
shop'.



---
Chapter 2 : A Mission to fetch a a Cornflower Spetum and kill a
harpy
---

And then he went on a mission to fetch a Cornflower Spetum. He
went to Hwczvlr and killed a harpy. On the body, he found
Japanese Poet book and Sidewalk Chalk bar.



---
Chapter 3 : The feast of the hydra
---

And hast thou killed the hydra, my daughter? Calloo! Callay! We
must have a feast!

The first course was hors d'oeuvre. It consisted of tapas.

The second course was soup. It consisted of Sliced fish soup.

The third course was hors d'oeuvre. It consisted of deep fried
ravioli and paneer tikka.

The fourth course was salad. It consisted of a simple
presentation of endive topped with croutons.

The fifth course was soup. It consisted of Borscht.

The sixth course was entree. It consisted of pickled and salted
peacock.

The seventh course was salad. It consisted of a simple
presentation of mâche topped with lite ranch dressing and
italian dressing.

The eighth course was entree. It consisted of seared whale.

The ninth course was soup. It consisted of French onion soup.

The tenth course was soup. It consisted of Cream of celery.

The eleventh course was soup. It consisted of Šaltibarščiai.

The twelfth course was hors d'oeuvre. It consisted of onion
rings and carpaccio.

The thirteenth course was crudite. It consisted of cucumber
sticks, carrots, cucumber slices, and cauliflower.

The fourteenth course was crudite. It consisted of red bell
pepper strips, baby carrots, parsnips, and parsnips.

The fifteenth course was dessert. It consisted of vanilla
pudding.

The sixteenth course was dessert. It consisted of Linga.

The seventeenth course was dessert. It consisted of port.

The final course was dessert. It consisted of shortbread.

Chapter 6 : The feast of the human
---

And hast thou killed the human, my daughter? Calloo! Callay! We
must have a feast!

The first course was salad. It consisted of oakleaf, spinach,
and frisée topped with roasted pumpkin seeds.

The second course was entree. It consisted of charred and
charred dolphin, stuffed inside a charred and boiled pork.

The third course was entree. It consisted of salted duck, topped
with egusi sauce.

The fourth course was hors d'oeuvre. It consisted of potato
chips.

The fifth course was soup. It consisted of Bergen fish soup.

The sixth course was salad. It consisted of a simple
presentation of butter lettuce topped with sunflower seeds and
roasted pumpkin seeds, drizzled with thousand island dressing.

The seventh course was salad. It consisted of tatsoi, spinach,
and escarole topped with black beans, black beans, and croutons.

The eighth course was salad. It consisted of a simple
presentation of arugala topped with lite ranch dressing.

The ninth course was dessert. It consisted of port.

The final course was dessert. It consisted of madeira.

Chapter 9 : The feast of the floating eye beast
---

And hast thou killed the floating eye beast, my daughter?
Calloo! Callay! We must have a feast!

The first course was salad. It consisted of bibb lettuce, butter
lettuce, and radicchio topped with sesame seeds and sunflower
seeds.

The second course was crudite. It consisted of asparagus spears,
red bell pepper strips, cucumber wedges, and red bell pepper
strips.

The third course was entree. It consisted of raw and grilled
giraffe.

The fourth course was crudite. It consisted of carrots,
cauliflower, broccoli, and baby carrots.

The fifth course was salad. It consisted of a simple
presentation of elf herb topped with peppercorn ranch dressing,
sunflower seeds, and corn strips.

The sixth course was salad. It consisted of oakleaf and cress
topped with sesame seeds, corn strips, and sunflower seeds.

The seventh course was crudite. It consisted of celery,
cauliflower, celery, and asparagus spears.

The eighth course was salad. It consisted of green leaf lettuce,
red leaf lettuce, and endive topped with blue cheese dressing,
sunflower seeds, and wonton strips.

The ninth course was soup. It consisted of Melon soup.

The tenth course was hors d'oeuvre. It consisted of garlic knot
and pizza pockets.

The eleventh course was soup. It consisted of Nikujaga.

The twelfth course was hors d'oeuvre. It consisted of chaat and
nachos.

The thirteenth course was soup. It consisted of Seafood chowder.

The fourteenth course was dessert. It consisted of birthday
cake.

The final course was dessert. It consisted of gelato.

Chapter 14 : A Mission to fetch a a Blue Grouse bo and kill a
hydra
---

And then he went on a mission to fetch a Blue Grouse bo. He went
to Widqbu and killed a hydra. On the body, he found Rose Dust
grail and Wheatacre scroll.



---
Chapter 15 : The feast of the ooze
---

And hast thou killed the ooze, my daughter? Calloo! Callay! We
must have a feast!

The first course was entree. It consisted of dried bear, stuffed
inside a raw salmon.

The second course was crudite. It consisted of radishes, green
bell pepper strips, cucumber wedges, and celery.

The third course was crudite. It consisted of baby carrots, red
bell pepper strips, celery, and parsnips.

The fourth course was entree. It consisted of pressed
rhinocerous, topped with biryani sauce.

The fifth course was crudite. It consisted of radishes,
cauliflower, parsnips, and broccoli.

The sixth course was soup. It consisted of Snert.

The seventh course was soup. It consisted of Bacon soup.

The eighth course was hors d'oeuvre. It consisted of fritos.

The ninth course was soup. It consisted of Lung fung soup.

The tenth course was dessert. It consisted of gelatin dessert.

The final course was dessert. It consisted of birthday cake.

Chapter 30 : A Mission to fetch a a Rhapsody Rap long sword and
kill a zyqxuwy
---

And then he went on a mission to fetch a Rhapsody Rap long
sword. He went to Fkaax and killed a zyqxuwy. On the body, he
found Mondrian Blue bar and Mud Berry Quarter bar.



---
Chapter 31 : The feast of the zyqxuwy
---

And hast thou killed the zyqxuwy, my daughter? Calloo! Callay!
We must have a feast!

The first course was hors d'oeuvre. It consisted of rocky
mountain oysters and salmon nigiri.

The second course was soup. It consisted of White veal.

The third course was soup. It consisted of French onion soup.

The fourth course was soup. It consisted of Soto ayam.

The fifth course was salad. It consisted of a simple
presentation of spinach topped with black beans and black beans.

The sixth course was soup. It consisted of Pumpkin.

The final course was dessert. It consisted of trifle.

Chapter 34 : The feast of the kobold
---

And hast thou killed the kobold, my daughter? Calloo! Callay! We
must have a feast!

The first course was crudite. It consisted of fennel, green bell
pepper strips, red bell pepper strips, and broccoli.

ram, topped with butter chicken sauce.

celery, parsnips, and baby carrots.

served with yellow curry sauce, Garlic sauce, and barbecue
sauce.

The fifth course was soup. It consisted of Leek soup.

The final course was dessert. It consisted of banana pudding.

Chapter 37 : The feast of the hydra
---

And hast thou killed the hydra, my daughter? Calloo! Callay! We
must have a feast!

The first course was salad. It consisted of frisée and green
leaf lettuce topped with croutons and croutons, drizzled with
lite ranch dressing.

The second course was salad. It consisted of butter lettuce
tossed with kale topped with black beans, italian dressing, and
sunflower seeds.

The third course was entree. It consisted of salted
hippopotamus, topped with romesco.

The fourth course was crudite. It consisted of red bell pepper
strips, cucumber sticks, celery, and green bell pepper strips.

The fifth course was salad. It consisted of a simple
presentation of cress topped with wonton strips.

The sixth course was hors d'oeuvre. It consisted of meze.

The seventh course was soup. It consisted of żur.

The eighth course was hors d'oeuvre. It consisted of fried
mushrooms and meze.

The ninth course was salad. It consisted of green leaf lettuce
and frisée topped with corn strips.

The tenth course was entree. It consisted of pickled man.

The eleventh course was entree. It consisted of jerked and
grilled wren, topped with Tkemali.

The twelfth course was salad. It consisted of baby beet greens,
kale, and frisée topped with corn strips, blue cheese dressing,
and blue cheese dressing.

The thirteenth course was crudite. It consisted of baby carrots,
baby carrots, parsnips, and radishes.

The fourteenth course was soup. It consisted of Joumou.

The fifteenth course was dessert. It consisted of ice cream.

The final course was dessert. It consisted of blueberry soup.

Chapter 40 : The feast of the ooze
---

And hast thou killed the ooze, my daughter? Calloo! Callay! We
must have a feast!

The first course was crudite. It consisted of green bell pepper
strips, cucumber slices, fennel, and celery.

The second course was entree. It consisted of grilled back
bacon, topped with Béchamel.

The third course was crudite. It consisted of radishes, celery,
fennel, and baby carrots.

The fourth course was hors d'oeuvre. It consisted of shrimp
cocktail.

The fifth course was hors d'oeuvre. It consisted of gravlax and
carpaccio.

The sixth course was soup. It consisted of Vegetable soup.

The seventh course was entree. It consisted of raw and pressed
dog, stuffed inside a jerked elephant.

The eighth course was dessert. It consisted of chocolate
pudding.

The final course was dessert. It consisted of vanilla pudding.
